\Hypertarget{fsglbvar_8h_a8cf96cd117edbf9f1bced229d354ec2f}\label{fsglbvar_8h_a8cf96cd117edbf9f1bced229d354ec2f} 
\index{fsglbvar.h@{fsglbvar.h}!ConvertActualTimeToSimtime@{ConvertActualTimeToSimtime}}
\index{ConvertActualTimeToSimtime@{ConvertActualTimeToSimtime}!fsglbvar.h@{fsglbvar.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ConvertActualTimeToSimtime()}{ConvertActualTimeToSimtime()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily double Convert\+Actual\+Time\+To\+Simtime (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{long}]{mo,  }\item[{long}]{dy,  }\item[{long}]{hr,  }\item[{long}]{mn,  }\item[{bool}]{From\+Condit }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Converts a time expressed in "{}component form"{} (ie\+: month, day, hour, minutes) to the same time expressed in minutes from the beginning of the simulation. ~\newline
 

This algorithm assumes that the arguments have the following units\+:

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item mo "{}month of year"{} number (1-\/12) \item dy "{}day of month"{} number (1-\/31) \item hr "{}hour of day times 100"{} number (0000 -\/ 2400) \item min "{}minute of hour"{} number (0-\/59)\end{DoxyItemize}
This algorithm works by converting the simulation start time to "{}minutes since the start of the year"{} for a reference. Then the provided time is also converted to "{}minutes since the start of the year."{} The "{}simulation time"{} is then computed by a simple subtraction of the start time from the provided time. ~\newline


Because there is no provision for specifying the year of any of the times, certain assumptions must be made. For instance, if the "{}month"{} of the provided time is less than the month of the simulation start, the algorithm assumes that the provided time refers to a time in the next year.
